  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer16612947993672844481">Olivia Kaspen has just discovered that her ex-boyfriend, Caleb Drake, has lost his memory. With an already lousy reputation for taking advantage of situations, Olivia must decide how far she is willing to go to get Caleb back. Wrestling to keep her true identity and their sordid past under wraps, Olivia’s greatest obstacle is Caleb’s wicked, new girlfriend; Leah Smith. It </span>
  <span id="freeText16612947993672844481" style="display:none">Olivia Kaspen has just discovered that her ex-boyfriend, Caleb Drake, has lost his memory. With an already lousy reputation for taking advantage of situations, Olivia must decide how far she is willing to go to get Caleb back. Wrestling to keep her true identity and their sordid past under wraps, Olivia’s greatest obstacle is Caleb’s wicked, new girlfriend; Leah Smith. It is a race to the finish as these two vipers engage in a vicious tug of war to possess a man who no longer remembers them. But, soon enough Olivia must face the consequences of her lies, and in the process discover that sometimes love falls short of redemption.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16612947993672844481" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>

</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<div class='spoiler'>
This answer contains spoilers…
<span class='spoilerAnswerText'>
<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  
    Well both characters sleep with other people. But technically there is no cheating. They only sleep with other people when they are not together. Howe<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">…more</a>
    Well both characters sleep with other people. But technically there is no cheating. They only sleep with other people when they are not together. However, there is a scene when Olivia catches Caleb with another woman in his office, it is made to look like cheating. But you find out that in the third book he wasn't cheating on her. But she assumes and leaves.<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>
  
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer330717549" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3447981965135792250">Wow! I needed a minute to collect my thoughts after this one. This book was recommended to me by a friend that said—-<i>you have to read this so we can talk about it!</i> I glanced over the reviews, and after seeing a sea of shouty capitals and exclamation points, I thought, she’s right, I need to read this!<br/><br/>I am so glad I did!<br/><br/>First off, the descriptive turn of phrases in this book made me smile. Every other paragraph had something in it that made me take notice. Even the hard parts were a joy to read—-</span>
  <span id="freeText3447981965135792250" style="display:none">Wow! I needed a minute to collect my thoughts after this one. This book was recommended to me by a friend that said—-<i>you have to read this so we can talk about it!</i> I glanced over the reviews, and after seeing a sea of shouty capitals and exclamation points, I thought, she’s right, I need to read this!<br /><br />I am so glad I did!<br /><br />First off, the descriptive turn of phrases in this book made me smile. Every other paragraph had something in it that made me take notice. Even the hard parts were a joy to read—-which is saying something, because there are some REALLY hard parts in this!<br /><br />Second…Olivia, Olivia, Olivia. I loved her and I felt like I understood her and her issues. I also wanted to shake her and scream some sense into her too! I wanted to magically heal her, show her what her life could be, and then set her loose to happily walk into the sunset. But she needed the journey she went through, as painful as it was.<br /><br />And lastly, Caleb. Wow, I think I love this man. Is he perfect? Heck no! Did I like all of his choices? Definitely not! But I love him regardless. Some of the scenes between Caleb and Olivia will be staying with me for a very long time, the good ones and the bad ones.<br /><br />I can’t say that I loved how it ended, but I understand it…sort of. I’m still working it out in my head, actually. But I think that what happened needed to happen for the sake of the characters. Olivia especially. That being said, I also don’t see the ending as being <i>the end</i>. In my mind, there is more, so much more! I only hope that someday the fantabulous Tarryn Fisher will agree with me! Please?<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3447981965135792250" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText10665044319037994934" style="display:none">Author Interview <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://toughcriticbookreviews.blogspot.com/2012/05/interview-giveaway.html">http://toughcriticbookreviews.blogspo...</a><br /><br />EFFITY, EFF, EFF!!! EVERY. SINGLE. EFFING. ONE. Hell, this entire review could be written in shouty capitals!!<br /><br />This book metamorphosed my entire existence! <div id="review_390641968" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/390641968" />
    <a title="C.J. Roberts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5824154-c-j-roberts"><img alt="C.J. Roberts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442603851p2/5824154.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/390641968?book_show_action=true">Aug 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.J. Roberts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.J. Roberts" href="/user/show/5824154-c-j-roberts">C.J. Roberts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Lovers of Captive in the Dark</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to C.J. by: </span>
      Tarryn Fisher
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5824154-c-j-roberts?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5824154-c-j-roberts?shelf=indie">indie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5824154-c-j-roberts?shelf=get-out-of-my-head">get-out-of-my-head</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer390641968" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17807065934416287018">It started with a post from one of my readers on Facebook talking about Caleb and Olivia. I thought they were talking about my book so I checked it out, NOPE, they were discussing a different Caleb and Olivia. <br/><br/>I had to investigate.<br/><br/>THEN, Tarryn and I were both invited to be a part of the 2012 TFEiC Author Meet & Greet in Chicago. We struck up a conversation and it was effortless. We decided to do a buddy read of one another's books.<br/><br/>The more I read, The Opportunist, the more I thought: "This b***h</span>
  <span id="freeText17807065934416287018" style="display:none">It started with a post from one of my readers on Facebook talking about Caleb and Olivia. I thought they were talking about my book so I checked it out, NOPE, they were discussing a different Caleb and Olivia. <br /><br />I had to investigate.<br /><br />THEN, Tarryn and I were both invited to be a part of the 2012 TFEiC Author Meet &amp; Greet in Chicago. We struck up a conversation and it was effortless. We decided to do a buddy read of one another's books.<br /><br />The more I read, The Opportunist, the more I thought: "This b***h is squatting in my brain."<br /><br />Same character names (wow), our Caleb's are both blond (ok), our Livvie's are both brunette (interesting...), our Caleb's don't remember their pasts (get the F out of here!). And...WE HAVE THE SAME SENSE OF HUMOR!<br /><br />From The Opportunist: "He chuckles at me. I envision myself jamming a pen into his trachea. Blood. There would be lots of blood to clean up. I better not."<br /><br />From my Facebook page: "That awkward moment when someone is pissing you off and they have no idea you're perfectly capable of murder...awesome."<br /><br />Okay, so enough about how Tarryn is my suspect zero.<br /><br />I LOVED THE BOOK! Not for its similarities to mine, but for its differences. Tarryn's, Olivia, is conniving and manipulative - but also incredibly honest. I loved that. Most people are selfish, but refuse to admit it. Olivia put it right out there.<br /><br />I love that Caleb wasn't perfect. NONE of Tarryn's characters are perfect - they are human.<br /><br />There's been some talk about the ending and let me put my two cents in: This story ended exactly as it should. To suggest otherwise is to miss the point of the story in its entirety. This is not a book about two people falling in and out of love before they 'get it right'. This is a story about personal growth and finding the true meaning of love, which is: Loving someone means putting their needs above your own.<br /><br />Well done, Tarryn. I can't wait to see you in Chicago and stare into your eyes for the part of my soul you seem to have sucked straight from my mouth as I slept comfortably in my bed as a baby. The force is strong with you. I look forward to doing battle, cuz I'm a MIND NINJA!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17807065934416287018" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_672629675" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/672629675" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/672629675?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17846015-the-opportunist">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=book-1-of-my-fav-series">book-1-of-my-fav-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer672629675" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1679982515865153518"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429893i/861590._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407009ra/794627.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> What a beautiful, broken mess. <br/><br/><em>The Opportunist</em> was both a breath of fresh air and a sucker punch to the gut. 5+ stars!!<br/><br/>I loved every single word and yet few books have ever made me so incredibly frustrated. It was a phenomenally well-crafted, multilayered story about complex, flawed characters. It owned me. It made me want to scream and cry. It made me <em>feel</em>. It was devastating, heart-breaking and yet utterly addictive. It was honestly one of the best books I have <em>ever</em> read. It grabbed a hold of</b></span>
  <span id="freeText1679982515865153518" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429893i/861590._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407009ra/794627.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> What a beautiful, broken mess. <br><br><em>The Opportunist</em> was both a breath of fresh air and a sucker punch to the gut. 5+ stars!!<br><br>I loved every single word and yet few books have ever made me so incredibly frustrated. It was a phenomenally well-crafted, multilayered story about complex, flawed characters. It owned me. It made me want to scream and cry. It made me <em>feel</em>. It was devastating, heart-breaking and yet utterly addictive. It was honestly one of the best books I have <em>ever</em> read. It grabbed a hold of my heart and didn't let go.</b><br><br>But... before the actual review, you should know that as a reader I like functional couples. Separation makes me twitchy, cheating makes me queasy, and miscommunication makes me want to breathe into a paper bag. So... having heard about this book, I was scared out of my ever-loving mind, terrified even, to start it because it pretty much has every single thing in it that I usually dislike. I was seriously worried that I would flat-out, no holds bared <em>hate</em> it. <br><br>I couldn't have been more wrong. I <i> loved </i> it!<br><br>That being said, on more than one occasion I came dangerously close to dashing my Kindle against the wall in frustration and watching it shatter along with my heart but... *holds up one finger* ... the story was so well written and the characters were so compelling that I couldn't help but fall in love with it.<br><br>Tarryn Fisher is a master of words and a genius at manipulating the emotions of her readers. Reading this book is like watching a train wreck - you know what's coming and but you're absolutely unable to look away.<br><br>Ok. Where to start?<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I am Olivia Kaspen, and if I love something I rip it from my life. Not intentionally... not unintentionally either."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br>This story follows Olivia. This girl is just full of the most intense tangle of self-doubt and lack of self-worth imaginable. In college she fell in love with a boy and we're talking head over heels, once-in-a-lifetime <em>love</em>. But she was unable to admit it and the power he had over her heart terrified her so even though it went against everything she wanted deep down, she walked away.<br><br>Three years later, she finds out that Caleb, the man she still loves and who still owns her heart, has lost his memory in an accident and she sees this as the perfect opportunity to try and start over. This could be her redo, a chance to wash away the mistakes of the past.<br><br>But nothing is ever that simple. He has a life that he's built since she left and a girlfriend now too, Leah, who is determined not to lose the man she now loves. He may not remember his life but it's there looming over them and Olivia is racing against time trying desperately to rebuild what they'd lost knowing that at any minute, he could remember everything.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"After three long years, I have what I want and it isn't real. He doesn't know who I am, and if he did, he wouldn't be sitting in my living room... He doesn't remember me. How could you forget someone you loved even if I did rip his heart to shreds?"</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br>The story is told almost completely from Olivia's point of view in a mixture of both present day scenes and flashbacks to when they first met so we got to see both their interactions now as well as the build up to the tangled mess they were in before his accident.<br><br>They'd met in college. He was the jock who had girls flocking to him left, right and center and she was the girl with no intention of becoming another notch on his bedpost.<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>"I certainly didn't care what effect he had on the females on campus. Caleb Drake meant nothing to me. He would never mean anything to me. I was un-shmoozable. The end."</em>
</blockquote><br><br>She was so sure she had him pegged and yet at every step, this relentless, gorgeous boy seemed one step ahead of her...<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>"Do you take compliments?" he asked...</em>
  <br>
  <em>"If they're original."</em>
  <br>
  <em>He snickered and rolled his eyes.</em>
  <br>
  <em>"Okay, okay," he said. He was trying not to laugh... "Do you want the jock to compliment you or the guy who reads Great Expectations."</em>
</blockquote><br><br>I couldn't help but root for them. I wanted them to work it out and knowing that things between them had fallen apart in the future made everything that much more painful. I don't want to say more about the story for now but just know that it kept me riveted right up until the end. <b> Absolutely unputdownable. </b><br><br>Tarryn Fisher's writing is just phenomenal. This is such a well-crafted book. I honestly would have enjoyed reading it just for the writing alone regardless of how the story turned out. The wording, the flow of the story, it was just totally captivating and absorbing. By the end of the first page, my heart was 100% invested in the story. It drew me in, grabbed hold and didn't let go.<br><br>With the way it's written, you are <em>right</em> in Olivia's head experiencing every thought and emotional right along side her. I really loved her character and while I wouldn't have done the same things she did, I could also totally understand why she did them.<br><br>I felt terrible for her. At times, I just wanted to shake her and at others, I just wanted to hug her because I could tell that what was going on with  her was almost out of her control. The issues left over by her past had a deep hold on her and despite what she wanted, no matter how <em>desperately</em> she wanted it, it was like she couldn't help but bring the pain onto herself by shutting out what she wanted most.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I was a relationship retard. I kicked, shoved, and punched people out of my life, so they never had a chance to hurt me."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br>And it didn't help that, as swoony as Caleb was, he pushed her too far at times and crossed too many lines. Given how difficult being in a relationship was for her in the first place, I could totally understand why she reacted the way she did even though I could also understand his frustration with how much she kept holding back.<br><br>I felt bad for her because in many ways, she was her own worst enemy and brought more pain on herself than anyone else did. It was tragic and heart breaking to see how little self-worth she had. It was like she had a self-destruct button that was constantly being pushed. But I didn't view her as being as bad a person as she thought she was. She was just a flawed, damaged, woman who wanted the man she was in love with with every fiber of her heart and soul but just had no understanding about how to handle her feelings or go about healthily getting what she wanted.<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>"It's the same guilt fame I've been playing all along, to be near Caleb regardless of the circumstances or cost. <em>Caleb, Caleb, Caleb."</em></em>
</blockquote><br><br>She was just so locked inside herself. I could see her struggling with her emotions. She was feeling them so strongly but on the inside only and she just couldn't make the leap to communicate them to him because of how much she feared the power that Celeb had over her heart.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"He watches my face in fascination. He's looking for a reaction, but my reaction is all on the inside where he can't see it... where I am hiding it."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br>Ok, now I just need take a moment to <em>scream</em> that I LOVE CALEB DRAKE!!!!!!!!! Omg. I love him with a serious intensity. Ok, I hate him a teensy tiny bit too, but that's all part of the fun. Protective, spontaneous, intelligent, and caring, he just made me melt. He was flawed, to be sure, that man was <em>not </em>perfect but still... my heart <em>bled</em> for him because he was just caught in the middle of this tumultuous storm of emotions and lies when all he wanted was the love a girl who just didn't know how to love him back in a way that showed.<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>"You're a good guy, Caleb Drake."</em>
  <br>
  <em>"A man is only as good as what he loves most, right? I flinched.</em>
  <br>
  <em>Hopefully, that wasn't true. I was about as rotten as a month old egg.</em>
</blockquote><br><br>But like I said, I was also frustrated with him because he didn't know how to be with her either. He pushed her too far at times instead of giving her the safety net she needed but on the flip side, he was nearly endlessly patient with her in certain other respects. But I think what angered me the most was how in the end, the reason she ended up walking away was in reaction to something <em>he </em>did and he couldn't see that. It frustrated me to no end. He was wrong and utterly oblivious to how much his actions devastated her.<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>
    <strong>"You will remember me every day for the rest of your life because I was the one and you threw me away."</strong>
  </em>
</blockquote><br><br>*sigh*<br><br>This book perfectly captures the feeling of first love - and I don't mean the starry rainbows and butterflies of the beginning of a relationship, I mean the soul-deep, rooted-in-your-heart depths of first love... the kind that can't be diminished even years of heart ache, betrayals and devastation. The kind you don't forget and can never replace.<br><br>These characters are just so deeply flawed but with the way the story is written, you can see why they did what they did. I felt like even things that I'd normally hate to read about in other books, I was okay with here because of how much I could understand where each character was coming from.<br><br>So now... about Leah. I didn't actually hate her outright. I tried to be understanding of her because it wasn't as though she'd come on scene when Caleb and Olivia were a couple. She arrived afterwards and fallen in love with a man who could never love her back the way she loved him because he would be forever in love with someone else. No claim she could lay on him - no jewelry or vows - would ever buy the piece of his heart that belonged to Olivia. And that was actually kind of tragic to me so at first, I tried to be understanding. I mean, don't get me wrong, I <em>hated</em> what she represented which was someone that stood in the way of the happily-ever-after of the couple I was rooting for and I hated things she did. But, when I tried to look at things from her perspective, yes, many of her actions were extreme bordering on unhinged but... I kind of understood her too.<br><br>She just wanted Caleb. Was that a crime? In romance-novel-world, sure, yes it is. But I can't really fault her for wanting to fight for him even though I wished she'd just vanish off the face of the earth. It was actually something else that happened in the story later that made me despise her because it showed another side to her that just made me ill.<br><br>The book wasn't quite as angsty as I expected at first and so here I was, totally wrapped up in the story, thinking I had a good handle on where things were going when the 70% mark hit and HOLY TWIST!! Oh. my. God. Shivers went straight up through me - neck to toes. I teared up. Couldn't breathe. Woah!!! And from that point on it really built. This is where the train-wreck analogy comes in because I knew how it would end but I could not look away.<br><br>The ending gutted me. It was a quiet pain. No sudden twist or startling conclusion but just the realization of an inevitability that had been building that was full of absolute, heart-wrenching pain. I wouldn't actually call it a cliffhanger because it didn't leave you hanging... it just didn't end with the characters where you wanted them. Not at all. Thankfully though there are two more books in the series and so the story isn't over yet.<br><br>But you know one of the other things I loved about this book was that it was ballsy. It went where few romance novels ever go. It crossed all sorts of lines most romance novels never cross and unapologetically trampled over every bit of my heart. But it made me <em>feel. </em>I loved that.<br><br>To any readers out there who haven't yet read this and are on the fence, I say <em>go for it!!!!</em> Just be tolerant. The whole story is a giant mess. Expect that. Just ride it out and enjoy the craziness!<br><br>Like I said above, this is one of the best books I've ever read. I swear, more than half my book is highlighted. The writing is just gold. Absolutely phenomenal. <br><br><b> It's captivating, heart breaking, and devastating at times and the characters are deeply flawed but... I still have hope.<br><br>I'm holding out for love to win... It has to.<br><br>Right? </b><br><br>5+ stars!!<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429835i/861407._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786137._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429893i/861591._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="1679982515865153518" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_622059757" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/622059757" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/622059757?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/24807243-the-opportunist">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=shocking-twists">shocking-twists</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer622059757" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10910612595241716490">I am still trying to get a handle on how I feel after reading this book. You know it's a great book when it stays with you and you can't get it out of your head. This is one of those books.<br/><br/>I've had this book on my TBR for a very long time and I just hadn't ever gotten around to it until now. I saw rave reviews from friends and a part of me was worried that it wouldn't live up to the hype. Now, I'm kicking myself for not reading this book sooner! It has blown me away!<br/><br/>I don't want to give too much</span>
  <span id="freeText10910612595241716490" style="display:none">I am still trying to get a handle on how I feel after reading this book. You know it's a great book when it stays with you and you can't get it out of your head. This is one of those books.<br /><br />I've had this book on my TBR for a very long time and I just hadn't ever gotten around to it until now. I saw rave reviews from friends and a part of me was worried that it wouldn't live up to the hype. Now, I'm kicking myself for not reading this book sooner! It has blown me away!<br /><br />I don't want to give too much away, but will say that it is an unconventional second-chance love story. The heroine, Olivia, gets a chance to reunite with her ex-boyfriend when they cross paths over three years after their break-up. Caleb is suffering from amnesia, following a car accident, and doesn't remember the way she broke his heart.<br /><br />Olivia isn't your typical heroine in that it is her imperfections that often make her endearing as a reader. She doesn't put up a front or deny her bad thoughts. She wants Caleb and is willing to use any means necessary to get him, even if she knows that their time together is short-lived. <br /><br />Add in the fact that Caleb had apparently moved on with a girlfriend that he can't remember, but who is desperate to keep him as well, and you've got plenty of drama to keep this story going. As crazy as some of Olivia's actions were, and believe me they were, Leah is operating on the same level. Both women were willing to go to some pretty drastic lengths to hang on to Caleb.<br /><br />Despite her stalker tendencies and manipulative actions, I found myself begrudgingly loving Olivia. I wanted her to be happy and my heart went out to her. The deeper the story delved into her background, the more I wanted this underdog to come out ahead.<br /><br />Conversely, I didn't fully appreciate why both of these women were so desperate to have Caleb. Sure, he was a good looking, nice guy, but I didn't understand the "wow" factor. Honestly, I was kind of pissed with how expendable Olivia seemed to be to him, right from the start. <br /><br />Anytime he didn't get the reaction he wanted from her, he froze her out entirely for months or years at a time. I thought his treatment of her was far worse, yet she was portrayed as the villain. I didn't get it. <br /><br />Aside from one terrible and manipulative thing that she did to a girl that he was dating in college, which ultimately ruined his relationship with that girl, I found her actions to be far less offensive than his. If you ask me, he was entirely to blame for their second break-up, and at least partially to blame for the first.<br /><br />Regardless of fault, I was completely enthralled with this story. The writing was exceptional, with humor laced throughout. I devoured this audiobook! I am reading the second book now and it is every bit as good as this one.<br /><br />If you've been on the fence with this one, read it! It isn't your typical, rainbows and unicorns story, but it is well worth a read (or listen). I highly recommend this book! <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10910612595241716490" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_432773164" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/432773164" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/432773164?book_show_action=true">Oct 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=emotional-rollercoaster">emotional-rollercoaster</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer432773164" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14380679603803143851"><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You can only give your heart away once; after that, everything else will chase your first love."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>~<br/><br/><i>
  <b>Love.<br/>Lies. <br/>More love.<br/>More lies.</b>
</i><br/><br/><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380352896ra/706299.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><br/><b>This book was AMAZING and UNPUTDOWNABLE but after finishing it I just felt emotionally EXHAUSTED</b>.<br/><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394093ra/758763.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><br/><br/>From the moment I started reading <b>The Opportunist</b>, it sucked me right in. I was unable to put it down and thank God I was on vacation so I was able to finish it in one day. <i>The Opportunist</i> is a story about love mixed with heartbreak and deceit. It is</span>
  <span id="freeText14380679603803143851" style="display:none"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You can only give your heart away once; after that, everything else will chase your first love."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>~<br><br><i>
  <b>Love.<br>Lies. <br>More love.<br>More lies.</b>
</i><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380352896ra/706299.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><b>This book was AMAZING and UNPUTDOWNABLE but after finishing it I just felt emotionally EXHAUSTED</b>.<br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394093ra/758763.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br>From the moment I started reading <b>The Opportunist</b>, it sucked me right in. I was unable to put it down and thank God I was on vacation so I was able to finish it in one day. <i>The Opportunist</i> is a story about love mixed with heartbreak and deceit. It is about the choices we make in life and the effect they have on our present and future...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I have finally accepted that there are consequences to every action. I earned them and they are rightfully mine. There is no time to make bad decisions. Every step is precious. The definition of living is mine." ~ Olivia</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>
  <u>Then</u>
</b> - Caleb and Olivia meet each other when they are both in college. He's the hottest, most popular guy on campus; she's the kind of girl who rather spends all her time in the library studying. She's an extremely beautiful girl, but because of the way she acts, people don't easily approach her. She's distant and constantly keeps her guard up around other people. That is until she meets Caleb...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Caleb was like a hurricane that swept through my life, stirring up things inside of me that I never knew existed. He is a longing I will never cure."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>They fall in love, but because of Olivia's secrets and lies, it soon becomes impossible for them to stay together. The situation escalates, they break up (and not in a pretty way!). <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I will love again, Olivia, <u>you</u> will hurt forever. What you've done is...you are worthless because you make yourself that way. You will remember me every day for the rest of your life because I was the one and you threw me away." And then he left.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>
  <u>Now</u>
</b> - Four years after they both separated their ways, Olivia suddenly runs into Caleb again. She's shocked and surprised to see the man who she once loved so much, <i>especially</i> since Caleb doesn't seem to have <u>any</u> idea who she is... Apparently he has been in a car accident a while before and now he suffers from a severe case of amnesia. With Caleb not remembering anything from their past, Olivia spots <u>the perfect opportunity</u> to start over and maybe win Caleb back! That is, if she manages to steal him away from his current new girlfriend, Leah.<br><br><br>Will she succeed? Or will her deceit and lies once again come in the way of them finally being together? <br><br><br>Well, <i>that</i> is for you to find out by reading this captivating and emotional story...<br><br><br>--------------------------------------------------<br><br><br><b>Caleb</b> - I loved him (although at times he was a sneaky bastard too) -<p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394093ra/758764.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"He was my crack. I could never get enough, and when I had him I was already thinking about when I could have him next."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>As I said earlier, Caleb was the kind of guy who could get any girl he wanted in the blink of an eye. But he didn't just want any other girl, he wanted Olivia and for that he was willing to fight. Most of the time he was really sweet and considerate and I loved him for being so patient while Olivia was having a hard time expressing her emotions. What I didn't get though <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[is why he would suddenly consider cheating on her (if he loved her so much) without confronting her first with the fact that he wanted more in their relationship. I didn't get why he just stood her up! (especially because it was the night they were supposed leave together on a romantic weekend!!) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Then there were a few other things he did that made me a little angry with him but overall, I understood why he decided to handle the situation the way he did. <br><br><br><b>Olivia</b> - I really liked her (although I certainly don't approve of everything she did) -<p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394093ra/758765.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br>Olivia constantly kept her feelings hidden from the people around her, in fear of getting hurt.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I was a relationship retard. I kicked, shoved, and punched people out of my life, so they never had a chance to hurt me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I often wished she would stop being so insecure and that she would be a little more open and honest about what she was feeling; I think that way she could have spared Caleb and herself a lot of heartbreak. On the other hand, by the second half of the story she did start to come through. She new what she wanted and she was willing to go a long way to get it. She was a master of the façade and she wasn't afraid to get her hands dirty.<br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I took it a step further, because remember, I fight dirty."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>I would never condone some of the steps she took to accomplish her way, but the way the author wrote it, I really felt a lot of sympathy towards her and I was constantly rooting for her so she could finally get the happy ending she deserved.<br><br><br><b>Leah</b> - All I have to say to her is -<p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394093ra/758766.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394093ra/758767.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br>Seriously, I <u>HATED</u> her!!! From what I've read of her so far, I can honestly say there isn't a good bone in her body. How she manipulated her way into Caleb's life is disgusting and I really hope she will finally get what she deserves somewhere in the next part of this series. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I kiss him for all the times I never got to kiss him, and for the times he's been kissing Leah instead of me. I kiss him because I ruined everything and I could have had this every day."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And after the way it ended, I just wanted to crawl in a hole and die.<br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380390080ra/751617.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Not that I'm such a sucker for a HEA (or maybe I am...) but for these two I really hope the future holds a lot more in store... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> (hopefully in the next part of the series!).<br><br>To everyone who hasn't read this incredible book yet, I would say <b>
  <u>READ IT</u>
</b>!!! It's an incredible story that will stay with me for a very long time. Even now, days after finishing it, I often still think about this book. <b>Tarryn Fisher</b> sure is an amazingly talented writer and I can't wait to read the next part of this series <u>very</u> soon!!!!<br><br><br><br><u>
  <b>Favorite quotes</b>
</u><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"And my favorite, your lips." He smiled as a pink flush crept up my neck. "Full and sensual, pluckered, and always turned down at the corners. They kind of make me want to kiss them until they smile."<br><br>~~~<br><br>"There is more to loving someone than just making yourself happy. You have to want him to be happier than you are."<br><br>~~~<br><br>"Life balances itself on a precarious ledge, we can stay safe up high or propel off the ledge."<br><br>~~~<br><br>"It's the last real kiss of my life. I forever cling to that kiss. It was goodbye and I'm sorry and I love you so much."<br><br><br><br>~~~<br><br></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>5 brilliantly complicated but beautiful STARS!!!</b><br><br><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="14380679603803143851" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_736644308" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/736644308" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/736644308?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Those who don't mind unlikable narrators</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=na-experiment">na-experiment</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=2014">2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer736644308" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18220631586691100166"><blockquote>
  <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/list/4622890?shelf=na-experiment' rel='nofollow noopener'>
    <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393006047i/8646654.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  </a>
  <br/>
  <br/>
  <i>
    <b>"Are you a bad person, Olivia?"<br/>"Yes," I say easily.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><u>This book was almost impossible to rate.</u> My mind literally feels like it has been torn in half over this book - and particularly torn in half over my opinion of the main character. There are a number of things you should probably know.<br/><br/>1) <b>The writing.</b> The writing in <i>The Opportunist</i> is a cut above many of the other New Adult books I've read. It's compulsively readable and extremely entertaining, to the point where I fi</span>
  <span id="freeText18220631586691100166" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/list/4622890?shelf=na-experiment" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393006047i/8646654.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
  <br>
  <br>
  <i>
    <b>"Are you a bad person, Olivia?"<br>"Yes," I say easily.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><u>This book was almost impossible to rate.</u> My mind literally feels like it has been torn in half over this book - and particularly torn in half over my opinion of the main character. There are a number of things you should probably know.<br><br>1) <b>The writing.</b> The writing in <i>The Opportunist</i> is a cut above many of the other New Adult books I've read. It's compulsively readable and extremely entertaining, to the point where I finished this novel in a single sitting and immediately considered picking up the sequel. There was a single cringy piece of writing somewhere near the beginning that made me roll my eyes, but it thankfully remained lonely and the rest was good. Here it is, because any small amount of respect my online friends have for me would disappear if I didn't point this beauty out: <i>
  <b>"He was like a jalapeño, bright and smooth, but dangerously hot. A small part of me wanted to bite him."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402153936ra/9900647.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>2) <b>The protagonist.</b> She is a complete bitch. I don't say that lightly, either. This girl is a manipulative, backstabbing, slut-shaming piece of work. She constantly screws people over to get what she wants. Being inside her mind is like receiving a constant stream of hatred towards every other person and especially every other woman.<br><br>But... she's kind of different to every other annoying, insufferable New Adult main character. Sure, she shares a lot of the same characteristics, but what I personally hate is the way many NA MCs treat other women with disdain as part of the author's mission to get us to view the MC in a positive "pure" way and other women as evil and "slutty". That isn't the case here. Olivia is an unlikable protagonist and the author never tries to sell her as something else. We know she's a bitch and we're meant to know, even Olivia knows it. <b>If you don't mind unlikable narrators, then you might actually love this book.</b><br><br>Take this quote from the lovely Olivia: <b>
  <i>"The thought of Leah in a white dress made me want to laugh. She was better suited for slutty lingerie and a stripper pole."</i>
</b> Damn, I hate her. I'm pretty sure T-Swift wrote a song about her...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402154495ra/9900678.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I hate her, but I strangely sympathise with some parts of her story. Olivia is so bitter towards everyone in her life that she screws up all her relationships, not just romantic ones. She is painfully alone. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I had taken advantage of a girl looking for someone to trust and I used her predicament for my own personal gain. I was my father’s child. I hated myself."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Olivia doesn't get what she wants and she has no one to blame but herself... I thought this was an intriguing spin on the more typical stories of a woman trying to get the man she loves.<br><br>3) <b>The story.</b> The plot alternates between the past and the present. A past Olivia falls in love with Caleb and proceeds to ruin the relationship with her own manipulative, self-destructive personality. In the present, Olivia runs into Caleb again, only to discover that an accident has robbed him of his memory. Seeing an opportunity, hence the title, Olivia pretends not to know Caleb and attempts to make him fall for her all over again before he gets his memory back and marries Leah - his red-headed girlfriend (and narrator of the sequel). <br><br>I thoroughly enjoyed reading about the development and downfall of the relationship, as well as Olivia's opportunistic ploy to win him back. Without giving away any spoilers, approximately the last quarter is set even further into the future and was actually pretty sad at points.<br><br>4) <b>The melodrama.</b> This is going to be a short point but Olivia is a self-confessed drama llama. Sometimes it tried my patience. I mean, come on, what even is this: <i>
  <b>"I make noises I will regret until the day I die."</b>
</i> Let's think about that a minute, shall we? You make noises in sex you will regret until the day you die. Noises... you will regret... <b>
  <u>until the day you die.</u>
</b> You obviously have way too much time on your hands if you can regret some noises until the day you die. I don't care if you break out into the Pokemon theme tune mid-orgasm, dude, you get over it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402156701i/9900936.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>5) <b>The love interest.</b> I have mixed feelings about Caleb too. In the same way, I feel like I understand a lot of his motivations even though I don't agree with everything he does. <b>Honestly, they're fucking perfect for each other if anyone is.</b> But I won't go into spoilers, so I will say that I liked him a lot more than many NA love interests. He's sweet, funny and romantic for the most part. Predictably beautiful, of course, but I suppose that comes with the genre. <br><br>Also, I'm a bit of a sucker for the kind of love stories that happen over a long period of time, with both parties meeting up and almost making it work but eventually being torn apart again... until next time. I know, I know, could the <i>When Harry Met Sally</i> influence be more obvious? <b>Shut up, I love that movie.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402156313ra/9900898.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>6) <b>The ending.</b> I liked it. I saw the earlier "twist" coming a mile away, though. But it didn't matter too much. I like how things were wrapped up well but left open for the sequel at the same time. It was perfect yet sad, and I'm glad things worked out that way. Despite my thoughts and feelings being all over while reading this, it had enough of an impact that I know I want to pick up the next book. And I'm interested in what Leah has to say. <b>Spoil this series in the comments and I will throw my Harry Potter hardbacks at you. You've been warned :)</b><br><br><a href="http://thebookgeek.co.uk" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.leafmarks.com/emilymay" rel="nofollow noopener">Leafmarks</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thebookgeekreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thebookgeek01" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/emleemay" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="http://mycountryheart.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="18220631586691100166" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_484477044" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484477044" />
    <a title="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha"><img alt="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528597635p2/15735368.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/484477044?book_show_action=true">Dec 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" href="/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha">SueBee★bring me an alpha!★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940013482746" href="/book/show/15706044-the-opportunist">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=series-g-contemporaries">series-g-contemporaries</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=epic">epic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=read-contemporaries">read-contemporaries</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=g-contemporaries">g-contemporaries</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=student">student</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=heroes-favs-modern">heroes-favs-modern</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=heroes-rich-all">heroes-rich-all</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=heroes-rich-heir-tycoon-modern">heroes-rich-heir-tycoon-modern</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=triangle">triangle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer484477044" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5930776065151680071"><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/FisherTheOpportunist1TitlebySueBee_zpsbab4b640.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401890i/780602.jpg' alt=' photo FisherTheOpportunist1TitlebySueBee_zpsbab4b640.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>★★★★★! Love Me With Lies, book 1 of 3! The epic and very dysfunctional love saga of Caleb & Olivia taking you on a roller-coaster of emotions!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“He will remember eventually and this whole charade will come crashing down around me like a bad game of Jenga. Until then, I have him back and I am going to hold onto that for as long as I can.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><b>The Love Me With Lies series is Caleb Drake’s and Olivia Kaspen’s whirlwind saga spanning over a decade</b> filled with love, joy, angst, a</span>
  <span id="freeText5930776065151680071" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/FisherTheOpportunist1TitlebySueBee_zpsbab4b640.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401890i/780602.jpg" alt=" photo FisherTheOpportunist1TitlebySueBee_zpsbab4b640.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★★! Love Me With Lies, book 1 of 3! The epic and very dysfunctional love saga of Caleb &amp; Olivia taking you on a roller-coaster of emotions!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“He will remember eventually and this whole charade will come crashing down around me like a bad game of Jenga. Until then, I have him back and I am going to hold onto that for as long as I can.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>The Love Me With Lies series is Caleb Drake’s and Olivia Kaspen’s whirlwind saga spanning over a decade</b> filled with love, joy, angst, anger, frustration, but mostly a <b>profound sadness for all the could-have-beens</b>. Their love, in all its dysfunction and deception, is so great it blurs the line between right and wrong, overcomes trial and tribulation with hopes of transcending time!<br><br><u>Books in Love Me With Lies series should be read in order and together:</u><br><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484477044" rel="nofollow noopener">The Opportunist</a> (book 1)<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/489144410" rel="nofollow noopener">Dirty Red</a> (book 2)<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/489144658" rel="nofollow noopener">Thief</a> (book 3)</b><br><br><i>My dear friend Ratherread shared with me that the author came up with the concept for the book while sitting at a coffee shop and thinking that if her ex came in with amnesia she would lie to win him back….</i><br><br>And so <b>The Opportunist (book 1) opens up... Olivia spots her ex, Caleb in a store</b> and decides to bump into him. When she discovers <b>he has amnesia she realizes she will do anything to have him back, if but for a moment,</b> until his memory returns. The story follows them in the aftermath of that meeting. It also looks back a few years giving us glimpses into how they met and the story takes as several years into the future. <br><br><b>The Opportunist is a love triangle told from Olivia’s POV</b> and it will give you a good understanding of who she is while Caleb remains a mystery and Leah makes her entrance as the villain. It will keep you glued all the way to the <b>shocking and painful ending</b>. Please be sure to have book 2, <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/489144410" rel="nofollow noopener">Dirty Red</a>
</b> handy!<br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/FisherLovemewithlies1-3HeroinebySueBee_zps51a1c7ec.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401890i/780603.jpg" alt=" photo FisherLovemewithlies1-3HeroinebySueBee_zps51a1c7ec.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Olivia Kaspen</b> frustrated me, while wrapping herself around my heart. Five words to describe <b>Olivia: Self-destructive, broken, insightful, endearing and lost</b>.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I’ll always want you, Olivia. It was never about not wanting you, it was about wanting you too much and you not wanting me back!”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/FisherLovemewithlies1-3HerobySueBee_zpsfb630566.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401890i/780604.jpg" alt=" photo FisherLovemewithlies1-3HerobySueBee_zpsfb630566.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>We got one little glimpse into <b>Caleb Drake’s</b> mind in this story, but for most part he will remain an enigma. Five words to describe <b>Caleb: Captivating, enigmatic, unforgettable, conflicted and enduring</b>.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Caleb had been my imperfection, with his slightly Americanized British accent, and the way he could play any sport and quote any philosopher. He was such a mix of class and jock, romance and jerk; it made me crazy.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>I can’t recall when last I felt such an urge to see a hero/heroine together, yet their story is far from over. <b>Spellbinding storytelling! Unforgettable characters! Unique plot! Epic! Epic! Epic!</b> Thanks Ms. Fisher! It was worth the wait!<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>You will remember me every day for the rest of your life because I was the one and you threw me away.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5 stars <br>Heroine rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 4 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 3.5 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 5 stars<br>Storyline execution rating: 5 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 5 stars<br>Story ending rating: N/A<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 4.5 stars<br>************************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 5 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this series: Yes.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Problems/girlrainbysb_zps7c89c53d.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_314707492" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/314707492" />
    <a title="Alexis *Reality Bites*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites"><img alt="Alexis *Reality Bites*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1404308282p2/5587514.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/314707492?book_show_action=true">Apr 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alexis *Reality Bites*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alexis *Reality Bites*" href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites">Alexis *Reality Bites*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">All Book Lovers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5587514-alexis-reality-bites?shelf=badass_heroine">badass_heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5587514-alexis-reality-bites?shelf=emotional-read">emotional-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5587514-alexis-reality-bites?shelf=stalker_or-stalker-habits">stalker_or-stalker-habits</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5587514-alexis-reality-bites?shelf=tragedy-tragic">tragedy-tragic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5587514-alexis-reality-bites?shelf=keep-u-up-all-night">keep-u-up-all-night</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5587514-alexis-reality-bites?shelf=heart_pounding_moments">heart_pounding_moments</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5587514-alexis-reality-bites?shelf=may-june-jul-aug2012">may-june-jul-aug2012</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer314707492" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13836467408817770180">Reader Beware this book will leave you screaming <b>"OH HELL NO"</b><br/>5 STARS out of 5<br/>Genre- Adult Contemporary Romance<br/>Setting- Miami, Fl., Georgia, and Texas<br/><br/>-Part one: Spoiler Free<br/><i>-'You can only give your heart away once, after that, everything else will chase your first love'.</i> - Inner thoughts of Olivia in The Opportunist<br/><br/><b>The Opportunist will penetrate the recesses of your being. <br/><br/>All due to CHOICES </b><br/><br/>The Opportunist is a book about choices- good ones, bad ones, small ones and big ones. Everything in our l</span>
  <span id="freeText13836467408817770180" style="display:none">Reader Beware this book will leave you screaming <b>"OH HELL NO"</b><br />5 STARS out of 5<br />Genre- Adult Contemporary Romance<br />Setting- Miami, Fl., Georgia, and Texas<br /><br />-Part one: Spoiler Free<br /><i>-'You can only give your heart away once, after that, everything else will chase your first love'.</i> - Inner thoughts of Olivia in The Opportunist<br /><br /><b>The Opportunist will penetrate the recesses of your being. <br /><br />All due to CHOICES </b><br /><br />The Opportunist is a book about choices- good ones, bad ones, small ones and big ones. Everything in our lives is built on the choices we make even the simple ones like to go left or right, to sit here or over there. Then we get the effect/conclusion these Choices bring. The effects can be joy, pain, violence, peace, salvation, destruction, love, hate all an abundance of answers to our choices. We encounter people whose lives can change from our Choices; and not all are innocent because they have choices too. In the end if you can stand by your Choices and live with them be thy great or small is up to you.<br /><br />In The Opportunist Olivia runs into the love of her life Caleb Drake at a music store. She thinks to herself "this can't be" she has not seen or heard from him in 3 years. When their eyes meet and she realizes he has no idea who she is because of his amnesia from a car accident she takes advantage. Olivia pretends she does not know him. Oh but she does know him very well, Caleb Drake her ex-boyfriend from college and former love of her life. Caleb Drake is tall, sexy, rich and has a British accent. Olivia hurt Caleb in the past and he walked out of her life vowing to move on and never look back.<br /><br /> Now once again unbeknownst to his former self Caleb is attracted to Olivia AGAIN. And the two strike up a conversation that leads to a friendship against Olivia's better judgement of course;) He tells her about the accident and his temporary amnesia. Olivia decides that she will keep him close for as long as she can. But Leah Caleb's girlfriend from before the accident decides she will not give up on their love easily. Leah fights for her man. Who will get Caleb in the end?? And is either worth the love he gives?<br /><br />The Characters<br />I swear Olivia had a self destruct button. Her inability to open up and let love in caused so much pain for others. She often refered to herself as cold. But she was bitter,a manipulator, calculating and sometimes just CRUEL. In my opinion she was not as cold as she would like us to think. Because a true cold person would have not felt a damn thing. Olivia felt things after doing wrong. She just chose to not allow others to see, she kept a facade. <br /><br />Caleb, i loved this guy. He loved Olivia all the way to the last page. He went through so much drama with her and his love overcame the bad. His choices played a big part in the books outcome.<br /><br />Cammie was hilarious she was Olivia's trusty sidekick to the very end.<br /><br />Leah was a surprise. Period. I had a love hate thing with her. She too was calculating and a manipulator. When she realized amnesia Caleb was falling for another woman she was not having it. She wanted Caleb and would stop at nothing to get him. I had to admire that.<br /><br />Phrase i loved the most "Priends" pretend friends. I ate that up.LOL!!<br /><br />My Ratings<br />Characters- Lovable and Cunning<br />Writing Style- Witty, Solid, Leading and Potent<br />Plot/Storyline- Heart Stirring, Soul Stirring and Intense<br />Overall- This book will penetrate the recesses of your being. READER BEWARE.<br /><br />For more reviews go to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a> <br /><br /><br /><b>Part Two: <br />SPOILERS AHEAD- READ AT YOUR OWN RISK BECAUSE I WILL NOT HOLD BACK! REPEAT, NOT HOLD BACK!</b><br /><br />My thoughts on the characters and the choices they made.<br /><br />Olivia was bold, calculating and ruthless when it came to getting her way and seeking revenge. It's like she had a self destruct button. But she then would have feelings of sadness for what she did. Like with Jessica that was by far one of the most cruel things i have ever read. Even though Jessica mad the decision to abort the baby. Olivia still had influence over the choice and she failed to choose the right one. Then when she decided to cash in her V-Card to some random guy. I thought i was going to rip my hair from my scalp.<br /><br />Caleb- He was leading... I love how the author played his position. He was not all good he was human he made mistakes. He put up with Olivia's closed heart until it made him act out. His choices were huge too. When he walked away after their first kiss i thought noooooo. It set off this chain reaction in Olivia that only brought them both pain.<br /><br />Leah- Red was a bitch. Period. But i liked her spirit when it came to getting Caleb back at all cost. Can't fault her for that. Right?!? Her whole deal with not paying for those people who died from the drug released by her company was not cool. I was not happy about that.<br /><br />Noah- Noah was a God sent altho i would not be surprised if Red had a private eye on Olivia and set her up with Noah too;) Noah helped Olivia grow the epilogue showed that Olivia had accepted things for what they were with the ability to move on and find peace.<br /> <br /><b>Okay for those who have read this book i would like to say that i for one was happy with the ending. </b><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13836467408817770180" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

However, if you are like me and like your “romance” with a twist of obsession and <i>zero</i> squicky </span>
  <span id="freeText4118152287687514193" style="display:none">Find all of my reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/">http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“Can I be your favorite girl?”<br><br>“You already are, Duchess.”</i>
</b><br><br>Dear Tarryn Fisher:<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/illinois/chicago/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442938018ra/16296100.gif" alt="Chicago commercial photographers" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It doesn’t have to be a snowman. Really, it doesn’t. We can just sit around and you can remind me that there are people who are even more f*&amp;^ed up than I am while I braid your hair.<br><br><b>WARNING:</b> If you like your romance fluffy with a HEA you best get to steppin’. However, if you are like me and like your “romance” with a twist of obsession and <i>zero</i> squicky sex scenes, <i>The Opportunist</i> is a good choice.<br><br>Let’s start at the beginning, shall we? Olivia met Caleb in college. She was the prude – he was the playboy . . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/illinois/chicago/" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>When Caleb set his sights on Olivia, she figured it was simply to be another notch on his bedpost, but a friendly wager led to one date . . . <br><br><b>

</a><br><br><b>WRONG!</b> Mitchell and I love unhealthy weirdies!<br><br>Fast-forward to the present where Olivia and Caleb’s paths cross once again. This time it’s different. Mainly because Caleb has a case of accident-induced amnesia, but Olivia ain’t ‘bout to look that gift-horse in the mouth so she decides she’ll take what she can get while she can get it and once his memory returns she’ll go back to being a broken-hearted shell of her former self . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/illinois/chicago/" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Ahhhhhh, tainted love. Momma likey.<br><br>The story does the wibbly wobbly from past to present in order to fill in the missing details. This is why I try not to get all . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/illinois/chicago/" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>when it comes to my practice of not reading past #1 in a series. <div id="review_477282368" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/477282368" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/477282368?book_show_action=true">Dec 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
