      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to ♥Rachel♥ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/1746727-arlene">Arlene</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer477282368" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10931722041477170845">One of the most addicting books I've read! Be prepared, you will not be able to put this down!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>I think that after the first time you give your heart away, you never get it back. The rest of your life is just you pretending that you still have a heart.</i>
</b><br/><br/>After reading a review of The Opportunist a while back I had planned on staying<i> far </i>away from this story. It sounded like drama and frustration, and I have little patience for either. But after my trusted friend Arlene <s>badgered</s> encouraged me to r</span>
  <span id="freeText10931722041477170845" style="display:none">One of the most addicting books I've read! Be prepared, you will not be able to put this down!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>I think that after the first time you give your heart away, you never get it back. The rest of your life is just you pretending that you still have a heart.</i>
</b><br /><br />After reading a review of The Opportunist a while back I had planned on staying<i> far </i>away from this story. It sounded like drama and frustration, and I have little patience for either. But after my trusted friend Arlene <s>badgered</s> encouraged me to read this, I had to give in. As I expected there was drama, (lots and lots and lots!) BUT there was very little frustration. After reading a few pages I was COMPLETELY hooked, and couldn’t put this book down. The story is riveting, and the writing was amazing! I’m currently pimping this story to anyone who’ll listen, so I’ll have more <s>victims</s> people to gossip with. <br /><br />Olivia and Caleb were together in college and had a horrible breakup. Actually, horrible is an understatement. The scars left a permanent mark on both of them, and continue to hurt even now. Olivia runs into Caleb years later and finds that he’s lost his memory. Initially, Olivia plans on just walking away and leaving things well enough alone, but she runs into Caleb a second time, and he wants to see her. Unable to resist the draw, Olivia starts seeing him again, all the while keeping the past a secret. She knows her days are numbered, because Caleb will eventually get his memory back, but she loves Caleb so much she’s willing to take what she can get. <br /><br />I have to say this story<i> utterly</i> consumed and HAUNTED me. If I had to use one word to describe this story, it would be INTENSE. We get this story in Olivia’s POV, and she is one passionate and obsessive character when it comes to life, but especially when it comes to Caleb. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>He was my crack. I could never get enough, and when I had him I was already thinking about when I could have him next.<br /><br />Caleb was like a hurricane that swept through my life, stirring up things inside of me that I never knew existed. He’s a longing I will never cure.</i>
</b><br /><br />Not that she lets many people see that. She has a wall as thick as Fort Knox around her heart, she’s so guarded. Even though you’re not in Caleb’s head you can tell he feels exactly the same about her. These two so desperately love and need each other, yet their manipulations and lies completely sabotage everything!! Normally this type of behavior would completely frustrate me and I’d want to chuck my Kindle across the room. This story was the exception. Tarryn Fisher so skillfully makes you empathize and feel for the characters, you can see why they do the things they do. <br /><br />Most of the time I find that alternating from the present to the past continually, annoys me. It didn’t here. I can’t gush enough about the brilliant way things were slowly revealed, ratcheting up the story a little more each chapter until the tension is about to <i>kill </i>you. My stomach hurt reading this, because I kept wondering when the bottom would fall out. <br /><br />My heart and head still hurt, and even though it’s days past since I’ve read it, I continually think about this story. I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15832316.Dirty_Red__Love_Me_With_Lies___2_" title="Dirty Red (Love Me With Lies, #2) by Tarryn Fisher" rel="nofollow noopener">Dirty Red</a>, the sequel the next day, in one sitting. As I said in the outset, my friend Arlene convinced me to read this. We attended a book convention this last weekend and all we did the whole time was gossip and theorize about this series! We convinced my husband to read this, too and he was right along with us in our obsession. I still can’t get this story out of my head. It was heart pounding, stomach clenching INTENSE, and I loved it!!! <br /><br />Right now this is a steal of a deal at .99 cents on <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Opportunist-Love-With-Lies-ebook/dp/B006FDAHZ4/ref=sr_1_1?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1359435969&amp;sr=1-1&amp;keywords=the+opportunist" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon.</a><br /><br />You can read this review and more at <a href="http://thereadersden.blogspot.com/2013/01/review-opportunist-by-tarryn-fisher.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Readers Den.</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10931722041477170845" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer2261364302483788972">I finished your book this morning, after having started it last night... I had to FORCE myself to STOP reading and go to bed. And even then, I was pissed that I slept when I could have been finishing this story.<br/><br/>This story HURTS. <br/><br/>H-U-R-T-S. <br/><br/>I'm still hurting. <br/><br/>Tomorrow, i'll probably still be hurting. <br/><br/>I'm sort of a jumbled mess of thoughts and emotions and even though I know what I FEEL about this book, i'm not sure how to actually SAY it. <br/><br/>This book is manipulative. The main character is a bitch. </span>
  <span id="freeText2261364302483788972" style="display:none">I finished your book this morning, after having started it last night... I had to FORCE myself to STOP reading and go to bed. And even then, I was pissed that I slept when I could have been finishing this story.<br /><br />This story HURTS. <br /><br />H-U-R-T-S. <br /><br />I'm still hurting. <br /><br />Tomorrow, i'll probably still be hurting. <br /><br />I'm sort of a jumbled mess of thoughts and emotions and even though I know what I FEEL about this book, i'm not sure how to actually SAY it. <br /><br />This book is manipulative. The main character is a bitch. She does things you'd never in a million years DO. Or maybe you would. Because you sort of understand why she's doing it. You get her behavior, her actions- no matter how screwed up they might be. And... and... I don't know. This book is messy. With lies, manipulation and angst throughout (not to mention some LOL lines of dialogue along the way)- but it's not an over the top cheesy romance with a happy ending all tied up in a perfect little bow (you know, the way mine are. LOL)... it's REAL. <br /><br />Too real. <br /><br />About how sometimes life is messy. Relationships are messy. People are messed up. We do stupid shit. We ruin things. We try to fix them. We run away. We lose things that matter. We want them back.<br /><br />It's hard to get them back.<br /><br />Life isn't always rainbows and butterflies. No matter how much I want them to be. It's not the truth. <br /><br />This book's truth hurts my heart. And when you read it (because really, how can you NOT?!?!) it will hurt yours too. </span>

    <a title="Dilek VT" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt"><img alt="Dilek VT" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448923258p2/49572641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1499931300?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dilek VT" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dilek VT" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt">Dilek VT</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=successful-writing">successful-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=beautiful-writing">beautiful-writing</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1499931300" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3140616378312088403">This review is about all 3 books in the series. <br/>Do not read these books as a stand-alone. They must be read in order.<br/><br/>*********************************************<br/><br/>This series is something else. They will (pardon my language but) f*ck with your mind! You will constantly be thrown away at the walls of an invisible torture room. <br/><br/>You will be made to feel and think something about someone. Love, hate, anger, pity, sorrow, whatever... <br/><br/>Then, you will be forced to change all these feelings and thoughts w</span>
  <span id="freeText3140616378312088403" style="display:none">This review is about all 3 books in the series. <br>Do not read these books as a stand-alone. They must be read in order.<br><br>*********************************************<br><br>This series is something else. They will (pardon my language but) f*ck with your mind! You will constantly be thrown away at the walls of an invisible torture room. <br><br>You will be made to feel and think something about someone. Love, hate, anger, pity, sorrow, whatever... <br><br>Then, you will be forced to change all these feelings and thoughts when the truth is revealed. <br><br>Just when you believe that you have the truth, you will soon see that it wasn’t really the truth at all. <br><br>Mind-f*ck, right? Yeah, that is what I am talking about... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459026954ra/18562471.gif" width="400" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The writer will play with your judgement, morals, assessment, your right and wrong. <br>The writer will definitely not treat you well.<br><br>*********************************************<br><br>I had these moments when I wanted to throw away my tablet, then bounce on it, jump on it, smash it into little bits and pieces. These series sucked the life out of me. <br><br>I seriously thought of putting them down, but that was impossible too, curiosity killed the cat, right?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459026954ra/18562472.gif" width="400" height="325" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, I managed to survive these books and now my life is given back to me after 3 days.<br><br>*********************************************<br><br><b>My final thoughts after completing the series: </b><br><br>This series, no matter how painful the process is, is definitely worth reading. They are extremely good. Just wait till the last sentence of the last book and you will agree with me. <br><br>Before that, you may be furious, angry, sad, depressed... But, it is worth the suffering. <br><br>*********************************************<br><br><b>This series is worth more than 5 stars.</b><br><br>The writing is very good. I had never read something like that before. Sure, there are many books around with flashbacks from the past. But this series is different. <br><br>All 3 books, have the same format: One chapter past, one chapter present, one chapter past, one chapter present. I don’t know how but the organization of it flows very smoothly and pulling this out requires great talent, I suppose. Congratulations to the writer...<br><br>There are main narrators for all three books and that changes only once or twice throughout the book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459026954i/18562473._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The first book is told by the heroine, Olivia, or the opportunist as the cover says. <br><br>I have been “Team Olivia” from the very start till the end unlike some readers. <br><br>At the end of this first book, I was so devastated, so miserable and so unhappy that for a moment I considered not continuing the series but then, I found the courage in myself to go on, and thank God, I did go on, or otherwise I would have missed a great reading experience.<br><br>*********************************************<br><br>The second book is told by Leah, the villain of the series, the snake or the dirty red as the cover says. You go from pitying her to wanting to murder her. That was some experience.<br><br>*********************************************<br><br>The 3rd book was the best of all. It is told by the hero, Caleb. <br><br>Up until the third book, I hated Caleb. I hated him for his mistakes, for what he did and for what he did not do. <br><br>In this third book, I understood him and made my peace with him. Then, I loved him. <br><br>Wow, from strong hatred to love...Go figure!<br><br>*********************************************<br><br>To cut it short, I recommend the whole series. Don’t miss them. They are a must-read. Not safe, but still worth reading!<br><br>I don’t want to go into plot details but it is about two soul mates who cannot have their happily ever after for an unbelievably long time because of their characters, their mistakes, other people’s interference and the fate itself... <br><br>It is not about second chances; it is about maybe tenth chances because the story is spread over ten years of a life time.<br><br>Read this series, you won’t regret it...<br><br>*********************************************<br><br>My favorite quotes from Book 1: The Opportunist:<br><i>
  <b><br>“I fell in love underneath a tree.” <br><br>***<br><br>“You will remember every day for the rest of your life because I was the one and you threw me away." And then he left.” <br><br>***<br><br>“Olivia, you can have any man you want. Why him ? Why is it always about Caleb ?" "Because...because I didn't need anyone until I met him.” <br><br>***<br><br>“Oh what do you know about love ? You've never cheated to have it.” <br><br>***<br><br>“Go be with your husband ... before he realises that he's still in love with me”<br><br></b>
</i></span>

<div id="review_349629907" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/349629907" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/349629907?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=drama-llama">drama-llama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer349629907" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9847842609496509213"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"From approximately twelve hours of knowing you, I have decided that I will never forget you, even if we never speak another word to each other. You leave a very strong impression. I can only imagine how that poor bastard feels after so many years of keeping company with you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>3.5 stars. That one quote sums up Olivia in a nutshell. Btw...I really liked Noah, the guy who stated the above. It's too bad we didn't meet him until the end of the book. He was quite lovely.<br/><br/>This book is not ab</span>
  <span id="freeText9847842609496509213" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"From approximately twelve hours of knowing you, I have decided that I will never forget you, even if we never speak another word to each other. You leave a very strong impression. I can only imagine how that poor bastard feels after so many years of keeping company with you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />3.5 stars. That one quote sums up Olivia in a nutshell. Btw...I really liked Noah, the guy who stated the above. It's too bad we didn't meet him until the end of the book. He was quite lovely.<br /><br />This book is not about the lovable Noah, however (why do I get the feeling that he's going to be playing the same role of Loring in How to Kill a Rock Star?). It's about Caleb and Olivia and their baggage - some extremely <s>fucked</s> messed up baggage.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I will love again, Olivia, <u>you</u> will hurt forever. What you've done is...You are worthless because you make yourself that way. You will remember me every day for the rest of your life because I was the one and you threw me away."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />Ouch. The truth hurts. Don't worry, I didn't actually spoil anything there...there's enough back and forth that you never really know what's going on with these two.<br /><br />At this stage of my reading life (yes, I go through stages), I am kinda-sorta over drama books. I fed off of these types of books in a gluttonous way for quite some time until they became nausea-inducing. This is probably why I put off reading <i>The Opportunist</i> for a while...I knew that I'd have to mentally be in a place to handle some drama.<br /><br /><b>How did the book work for me?</b><br /><br />It was entertaining. It was annoying. It was like looking into a mirror in parts. <br /><br />I am Olivia. I hated Olivia because <i>I am</i> Olivia. Rather, <i>I was</i> Olivia. Her games were all wrong, yet I've played some of those exact same games in past relationships. She deserved to have some major sense slapped into her, yet I understood (at times) why she acted the way that she did. <br /><br />At this stage in my life, I have no patience for Olivias. The mirror was hiding in the drawer in a nice, safe place. I was not having the desire to look in that mirror ever again. I suppose I should thank the author for that *fake rude glare*.<br /><br />In all seriousness, I was never quite as batshit crazy as this girl. She really did have a few screws loose. Caleb was no angel, but good lord, he was put through the ringer. I can't really fault him for trying to move on.<br /><br />I really don't know my feelings about this book. I liked it enough to rate it decently and am curious to read the rest of the series. However, I didn't love what was done to me. The book messed with my head just a little.<br /><br />Random side note : have you noticed all of my uses of the word "I" in this review? You probably haven't because you're nothing like me. This type of writing in <i>The Opportunist</i> drove me just a tiny bit crazy. Not enough to knock points off my rating but there were several sections where the majority of paragraphs or sentences started with I. Blame my business writing class for making me notice this but it's a big hurdle for me to have to get past when reading. The story was so engaging though, that this small issue was something which faded away after a while.<br /><br /><b>Should YOU read this book?</b><br /><br />If you can handle drama, sure...why not? Most of us could use a little mind screw every so often. If you're the type to want to slap someone for dishonesty and head games - run far, far away. Preferably at the speed of light.<br /><br /><b>My feelings about where the characters are headed?</b><br /><br />So...I'm a little worried. If this series ends anything like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1254951.The_Luxe__Luxe___1_" title="The Luxe (Luxe, #1) by Anna Godbersen" rel="nofollow noopener">The Luxe</a> series did (fabulous/beautiful/amazing story arc with WTF-ery aplenty at the end), I might have to punch someone in the face. <br /><br />Guess you'll just have to stay tuned to see whether I explode or not...</span>
  <a data-text-id="9847842609496509213" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1177437853" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1177437853" />
    <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader"><img alt="Aj the Ravenous Reader" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557800982p2/30248594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1177437853?book_show_action=true">Jan 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aj the Ravenous Reader" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader">Aj the Ravenous Reader</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=definitely-not-young-adult">definitely-not-young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1177437853" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12836686180404997634">My nostrils are still emitting remnants of smoke from my seething anger at the characters of this book. Sure, Ms. Fisher intended a story about flawed characters specifically about a ruthlessly manipulative woman named Olivia who would do anything for the love of her life; the playing womanizing “amnesia” diagnosed Caleb. But again, which character isn’t flawed. Aren’t they all are? But the things Olivia did to feed her whims are too heartless, too mean to even fit her supposedly blemished chara</span>
  <span id="freeText12836686180404997634" style="display:none">My nostrils are still emitting remnants of smoke from my seething anger at the characters of this book. Sure, Ms. Fisher intended a story about flawed characters specifically about a ruthlessly manipulative woman named Olivia who would do anything for the love of her life; the playing womanizing “amnesia” diagnosed Caleb. But again, which character isn’t flawed. Aren’t they all are? But the things Olivia did to feed her whims are too heartless, too mean to even fit her supposedly blemished character- a selfish opportunist. And what kind of opportunist would let her catch escape twice? Olivia being the narrator of the story confesses her actions which she perfectly knows are wicked and yet does them anyway drawing out from me countless number of eye rolls and headaches. In every cruel deed, she would ask herself “What would my mother say?” that I wanted to shake her and shout in front of her face, <b> “OH, PLEASE RECALL WHAT YOUR MOTHER SAID, YOU AREN’T THE ONE WITH AMNESIA, FOR CRYING OUT LOUD!” </b> Also, for a smart woman that she is, I’m surprised it took her seven years to understand what she really wants and who she really wants to be with. <br /><br />And then there’s Caleb- who Olivia describes as too good for her but I beg to disagree, because no- he isn’t good at all! He is a trickster, a player who controls her life without her knowing it. He changes girlfriends as often as he changes his trousers until he meets his match in Olivia. I couldn’t find even a pinch of sympathy in me for these two and even for the minor characters that are just as vile and hateful as these two. <br /><br />Now, now, why give it three stars then? Notice how long I’ve gone with this review already and still without gifs? Well, that’s how furious I am at the characters and it is for this reason that I give this a three star rating. For the author to be able to stir such a passionate though unpleasant emotion in me is an incredible feat! And I do believe that Ms. Fisher is perfectly aware of the effect of her characters on her readers and yet she boldly stuck to her stand and unleashed these evil characters upon her readers anyway. That was a very consciously bold move and I respect her for that and beyond because regardless of my ill feelings for the characters, I couldn’t deny the fact that this is one of the most coherent and most unified NA novels I have yet to read. <br /><br /><b> The plot </b>- composed of countless humps of unresolved conflicts inflicted by the narrator upon herself is just as erratic as the MC’ reason. <b> The shift of narration from past to present </b> connotes the unstable intentions of Olivia and even Caleb. <b>The fast pacing of events </b> implies one of the underlying themes of the story, which is <i> “the horrible consequences of hasty and thoughtless actions and decisions” </i> <b> The straightforward manner of writing </b> suggests the manner by which the story is concluded. So no matter how pissed I was at the MC’s, I am still logical enough to notice these incredible elements the author used to execute her story. <br /><br />On top of those that I mentioned, there is this one character- Noah whose part in the story was very little and yet most significant. He changed (at least a little) my opinion of Olivia and turned the story to something acceptable, even beautiful. Of all the characters, Noah was the only one who made perfect sense. <br /><br /> <i> Fight clean. Be honest. That’s the way you’ll win him back. But if you see that he’s happy, leave him be. </i><br /><br />What kind of ending do characters like Olivia and Caleb deserve? This is now up to you whether you’ll want to find out or not. ^^<br /><br /><b> This is one of those infuriatingly good books. ^^ </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="12836686180404997634" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_327728603" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/327728603" />
    <a title="Leslie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5433591-leslie"><img alt="Leslie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583458638p2/5433591.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/327728603?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Leslie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Leslie" href="/user/show/5433591-leslie">Leslie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5433591-leslie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5433591-leslie?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer327728603" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17159869084212607582">4.5 Stars!<br/><br/>When three of my GR friends were so emotionally drained after reading this book and couldn't rate it, or couldn't even review right away, I had to get to the bottom of it...immediately! I dropped everything and even "put-on-hold" a decent book I was already reading to find out. Boy, did I ever.<br/><br/>Alfred Hitchcock would have had a field day with this little psychological thriller, let me tell you! The camera angles alone would easily have been one of the main characters in his movie adapta</span>
  <span id="freeText17159869084212607582" style="display:none">4.5 Stars!<br /><br />When three of my GR friends were so emotionally drained after reading this book and couldn't rate it, or couldn't even review right away, I had to get to the bottom of it...immediately! I dropped everything and even "put-on-hold" a decent book I was already reading to find out. Boy, did I ever.<br /><br />Alfred Hitchcock would have had a field day with this little psychological thriller, let me tell you! The camera angles alone would easily have been one of the main characters in his movie adaptation. But, alas, this is just a book and a good one at that. <br /><br />Caleb and Olivia meet in college and they know immediately that their love is beyond anything either of them has ever felt before. Without giving too much away, this story is about way more than just the love between two obvious soulmates. It's about being young and immature, it's about selfishness, it's about loathing one's self so much it drives the other away; more than once. It's also about growing up and forgiveness, but never understanding and <i>or maybe denying</i> that pang in your belly you feel for someone, whom you think you can never ultimately have. <br /><br />The story began in the present, but took you to the past so many times; I was grateful that I committed to reading this quickly as it's not a book you can leave for a stretch of time and come back to without confusion. <i>Not that anyone could leave it for long...trust me!</i> This is a great, well orchestrated and impressive book. I'm giving it an extra star for the sheer brilliance of the continuous present and past timeline alone. I understand why it was an emotional book for the reader. It's tragedy, loss and manipulation will keep you on the edge of your seat and suck you in for a serious <i> yet sometimes gentle</i> roller-coaster ride.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17159869084212607582" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText11149494708154890694" style="display:none">Reread of a favorite book<br />#PopSugarChallenge2019<br /><br /><b>These characters are <i>deranged</i>. Mental, Psychotic, CUCKOO</b><br /><br />o_o <br />I found myself with my eyes wide a time or two while reading this.<br /><br />I am stuck between hating and loving this book. I really liked the weirdly dark intense manipulating drama, but at times it was just so much that it was unbelievable. This did not feel like a romance to me, it felt more like a psychological thriller. lol<br /><br />Olivia is a manipulative, broken liar. She is self proclaimed as "desperately wicked." She is a huge bitch and she knows it. She wasn't very likable, but I still found myself siding with her at times. I was rooting for her to be with Caleb. Why? I have no idea. <br /><br />I was really geared up for this secret to come out. I really couldn't put this down even though it was emotionally draining to get through all of the drama and stay inside Olivia's head. Fisher's writing is something I really enjoyed. She is totally screwed up but is brilliant. To know this book is part of her life makes it so much more wonderful. It was very unique, I like the dark side sometimes and she definitely delivered on that.<br /><br /><b>Life always keeps moving, even if it has to drag you along, kicking and screaming. </b></span>

<div id="review_2459843066" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2459843066" />
    <a title="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell"><img alt="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1584062476p2/2190064.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2459843066?book_show_action=true">Jul 17, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" href="/user/show/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell">Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17846015-the-opportunist">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=kissing-books">kissing-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=2018-romance-reading-challenge">2018-romance-reading-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2459843066" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1881663564590395265"><a href='http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Instagram</a> || <a href='https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twitter</a> || <a href='https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Facebook</a> || <a href='http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon</a> || <a href='https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Pinterest</a><br/><br/><br/>💙 I read this for the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/187063-unapologetic-romance-readers' rel='nofollow noopener'>Unapologetic Romance Readers</a>' <b>New Years 2018 Reading Challenge</b>, for the category of: <i>Second Chance Romance</i>. For more info on this challenge, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog_posts/16216645-urr-s-new-years-2018-romance-reading-challenge' rel='nofollow noopener'>click here</a>. 💙<br/><br/><br/><br/>A lot of my fellow romance-lovers enjoy cute, fluffy romances that make them smile. Not me - <b>I like my romance novels to make me feel like I've been sucker-punched in the solar plexus half a dozen times</b> before throwing me out on my ass in the middle of a busy sidew</span>
  <span id="freeText1881663564590395265" style="display:none"><a href="http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> || <a href="https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> || <a href="https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> || <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a> || <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a><br><br><br>💙 I read this for the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/187063-unapologetic-romance-readers" rel="nofollow noopener">Unapologetic Romance Readers</a>' <b>New Years 2018 Reading Challenge</b>, for the category of: <i>Second Chance Romance</i>. For more info on this challenge, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog_posts/16216645-urr-s-new-years-2018-romance-reading-challenge" rel="nofollow noopener">click here</a>. 💙<br><br><br><br>A lot of my fellow romance-lovers enjoy cute, fluffy romances that make them smile. Not me - <b>I like my romance novels to make me feel like I've been sucker-punched in the solar plexus half a dozen times</b> before throwing me out on my ass in the middle of a busy sidewalk. That's why I chose THE OPPORTUNIST as my "second chance romance"; when it comes to messed-up romance novels, Tarryn Fisher invariably delivers.<br><br><br><br>Our main couple, Olivia and Caleb, are epic trash people, and this is their saga of dumpster-worthy decisions. They first hooked up in college, but only after Olivia schemed, lied, and stalked her way into his heart, even going so far as to screw over his then-pregnant girlfriend by spilling out <i>all </i>of her dirty laundry. I saw a meme earlier that said "All Tea, All Shade" - that's Olivia. She's scandal wrapped in an ill-fitting dress. You can't quite hate her because her life is so awful, but you can't really stand to be around her, either.<br><br><br><br>It's told in dual timeline format, with the present story being written in present tense and the past story written in past tense, which can be a little confusing (especially since sometimes the author forgets which story she's telling, and slips into the wrong "tense"). This format is used to conceal information from the reader, because in the current story, Caleb, now with a different girlfriend, has amnesia, and Olivia, schemer that she is, takes advantage of his delicate condition in order to worm her way back into his heart a second time. We know that when they last parted, Caleb hated her for some unforgivable transgression, but we don't know what. All that we <i>do </i>know is that Olivia is one sick puppy... and as we read on, we find out Caleb is, as well. Maybe worse than we think.<br><br><br><br>The last third of the story gets extra weird and a little unbelievable, but I just decided to roll with it. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2193777550" rel="nofollow noopener">MUD VEIN</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2197096180" rel="nofollow noopener">MARROW</a> did the same thing. Tarryn Fisher seems to be making "jumping the shark" her trademark, and somehow she makes it work, even if you secretly admit to yourself that what's happening is a little stupid. The "past" story was the embodiment of virtually every negative new adult stereotype that I hate, but somehow Fisher made that work, too. I think it works because she doesn't try to apologize for being over-the-top or writing trash people characters. She just writes them and lets them tell their story themselves, rather than wasting time trying to apologize for them. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2222686995" rel="nofollow noopener">ATHEISTS WHO KNEEL AND PRAY</a> also featured a cast of incredibly repulsive characters, but I liked that book more than I should have, because it was compelling and unapologetic.<br><br><br><br>This definitely feels more unpolished than MUD VEIN and MARROW (both of which I believe were published later), and I noticed more errors in THE OPPORTUNIST, as well. There is also a higher rate of awkward metaphors that sound like something you might expect to see in a high school creative writing class, some notable ones comparing a dude to a shiny pepper she wants to take a bite out of and mouths clashing together like thunderclouds. *eye roll* But if you can get over the negative tropes and the unlikable people and the OTT drama, this is actually a riveting read. I devoured it in just a few hours and was frankly amazed at how quickly those pages turned. I own the two sequels and am excited to see what dark and reeking twisted alleys this story takes next.<br><br><br><br>3 stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="1881663564590395265" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/337342948?book_show_action=true">May 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer337342948" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5929676371281997236"><b>
  <blockquote>I am Olivia Kaspen, and if I love something I rip it from my life. Not intentionally…not unintentionally either.</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>When I first read the blurb, I wasn’t 100% sure that I wanted to read this. The whole premise is fascinating but I had already prejudged and tried Olivia and found her wanting before even giving it a chance. She’s not your regular every day heroine. In fact, how do you come to terms with the fact that the heroine of your novel is actually also the villain of the piece, the Cruella </span>
  <span id="freeText5929676371281997236" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>I am Olivia Kaspen, and if I love something I rip it from my life. Not intentionally…not unintentionally either.</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />When I first read the blurb, I wasn’t 100% sure that I wanted to read this. The whole premise is fascinating but I had already prejudged and tried Olivia and found her wanting before even giving it a chance. She’s not your regular every day heroine. In fact, how do you come to terms with the fact that the heroine of your novel is actually also the villain of the piece, the Cruella DeVille style antagonist of the story?<br /><br />The way Olivia conducts herself, her bitter and twisted inner monologue all makes for fairly uncomfortable reading. At first, I just didn't know what to make of her. After all, she is that character that normally hurts the main heroine in any other book, the one that threatens the special relationship with the hero – she’s the one we normally love to hate. But, oh boy, if I didn’t find myself completely absorbed by her and as the novel progressed, my reading speed picked up as I was so fascinated by what was going on that I just couldn’t put this down.<br /><br />Being inside Olivia’s head isn’t always a pleasant place to be but you know what they say about glass houses and who hasn’t found themselves consumed by jealousy over a hot guy at some point in their lives? Olivia is often selfish, frequently duplicitous and I came to think of her as Olivia The Deceiver but I did begin to develop a fragile respect and a bit of an understanding of why she behaves the way she does, her lack of trust and really start to ache at her pain and her inner turmoil. She’s far from perfect, more deeply flawed than most book heroines, but, in the end, she finally learns from the errors of the past and makes some fairly noble and selfless decisions and I ultimately came full circle and developed a deep affection for her.<br /><br />Caleb – well I just kind of loved him right from the get-go. He’s open, engaging, sweet, sexy &amp; funny – just about everything a good-looking, talented college jock should be. For the longest time he felt like an unknowing victim, desperately manipulated by the calculating women in his life and subjected to the most incredible pain by those that claim to love him. But, as this is very much a story of flawed and mostly confused people, it appears that Caleb isn’t always the saint I first thought he was.<br /><br />And as for Leah, Caleb’s significant other, well I just about loathed her on first sight but it pays to remember that she’s really not behaving any worse than Olivia and I’m erring on the side of caution and trying not to judge her for her actions as I know that we’re going to hear more from her POV in the sequel, Dirty Red.<br /><br />I think this whole story hinges on the theory that when you first fall in love and give your heart away, you can’t take it back and when you’ve met ‘The One’, everything and everyone else pales in comparison and just how far are you prepared to go to get what you want? At some point in all this, someone has to break the constantly repeating cycle of totally destructive behaviour and take a long cold look at what they are doing to themselves and everyone around them and take a tentative step in the right direction. <br /><br />So this was an incredibly compelling yet fairly challenging read. It’s not all neatly tied up with a pretty little bow on top – it’s edgy, taut, tense and wholly captivating. I have to say that I didn’t get the ending that I hoped for although I completely accept that it was the rightful and happiest ending possible. The whole book is tight with some real gasp out loud moments and shocks and unexpected twists in store. That pacing is flat out perfect as the story is told in dual time zones, both past and present, and everything is introduced at the right time and it all maps out beautifully. It’s meticulous story-telling and I flat-out applaud Tarryn Fisher for trying something refreshingly different with this trilogy and I am now moving straight onto the sequel because I just have to know………<br /><br />Totally loved it!<br /><br />4.5 stars<br /><br /><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a> or visit us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5929676371281997236" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_830066379" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/830066379" />
    <a title="Shell The Belle " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15880350-shell-the-belle"><img alt="Shell The Belle " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1399759491p2/15880350.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/830066379?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shell The Belle " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shell The Belle " href="/user/show/15880350-shell-the-belle">Shell The Belle </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">no-one, really</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15880350-shell-the-belle?shelf=guys-i-want-to-kick-in-the-balls">guys-i-want-to-kick-in-the-balls</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15880350-shell-the-belle?shelf=female-characters-i-want-to-slap">female-characters-i-want-to-slap</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15880350-shell-the-belle?shelf=what-the-hell-was-all-the-hype-for">what-the-hell-was-all-the-hype-for</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer830066379" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16108484425396720204"><b>2.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>WARNING UNPOPULAR OPINION TIME<br/><br/>Another one that just does not live up to the hype.</b><br/><br/><b>*Contains hidden spoilers but some minor ones are not hidden*</b><br/><br/><i>The Opportunist </i>is the first book in the <i>
  <b>Love Me With Lies</b>
</i> series, this one written in the first person from the female MC Olivia’s point of view. She tells the story of how she met her College love and how she lost him, only to meet up with him a few years later.<br/><br/>Well, what to say about this book, really? Not much. I didn’t absolutely hate it,</span>
  <span id="freeText16108484425396720204" style="display:none"><b>2.5 Stars</b><br><br><b>WARNING UNPOPULAR OPINION TIME<br><br>Another one that just does not live up to the hype.</b><br><br><b>*Contains hidden spoilers but some minor ones are not hidden*</b><br><br><i>The Opportunist </i>is the first book in the <i>
  <b>Love Me With Lies</b>
</i> series, this one written in the first person from the female MC Olivia’s point of view. She tells the story of how she met her College love and how she lost him, only to meet up with him a few years later.<br><br>Well, what to say about this book, really? Not much. I didn’t absolutely hate it, but I really didn’t like it. To be honest, it was all a bit, well, <br><br>Meh.<br><br>Lets start with what I <u>
  <b>DID</b>
</u> like about the book.<br><br>The story at the beginning had promise; I liked the idea of a college love lost, and then some years later fate brings them together again. I liked very much the storyline about Caleb, the male MC, suffering amnesia due to a car accident, and therefore there is a clean slate for the female MC to work with.<br><br>I liked the flashing back and forth from past to present; that was actually done really well and each chapter left you with a mini cliff hanger as it then switched from present to past and vice versa, leaving you eager to get back to each time frame to find out what happened next.<br><br>The writing style was brilliant. Tarryn Fisher really shows talent in the way she writes. I like this Authors style so far. <br><br>But the way the story unfolded? Well, it went on a bit, but what really got on my nerves was the dilly dallying of the two MC’s and their total indecision about each other.<br><br>What I <u>
  <b>DIDN’T</b>
</u> like.<br><br>To start with, as I said just, the dilly-dallying between Caleb and Olivia. I just did not see why? And we are constantly told, through Olivia that she (Olivia) is a bad person, terrible and rotten to the core, and that she did something really bad to Caleb, and that is why they broke up to begin with. But to me, when the whole part of that in the story is revealed, she is actually only half to blame. It seems as though she has to tell the reader over and over again how bad she is, and I just didn’t get it. Seriously, she tells the reader this <i>all the damn time</i> and yet she still does really bad things; so either she doesn’t care cos if she did she would stop, or its just attention seeking. <br><br>Throughout the whole series, I am screaming <b>“show, don’t tell”</b>.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=vxoy9d" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392487499i/8568266.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The one unforgivable thing she did, and this is bad, was to convince <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Caleb’s girlfriend in college to have an abortion, without talking to Caleb first. She knew this would split them up, you see, and it worked. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>And for the life of me, I just could not connect with either of the characters, especially Caleb.<br><br>Even during the flashbacks to the past, I didn’t like him and I just did not get their so-called chemistry or attraction. It just didn’t fit – I mean on their second date, she tells him she doesn’t think they will work, and instead of fighting for her, to try to court her and convince her, he just says okay and walks away! Then he gets involved with another girl, who he obviously really gets to quite like. So now Olivia does want him <b>*rolls eyes big time.*</b><br><br>The whole abortion thing was a farce, I mean, who does that to another girl? To convince her is one thing but to then make sure the whole college find out, just so Caleb will find out and break up with her over it? <i>
  <b>Am I supposed to like this thundercunt of a female character?</b>
</i> She has just ruined that other girl’s life at this point. <br><br>Olivia follows what seems to be the norm in YA/NA novels these days, and talks in a derogatory manner about other girls, calling them sluts, skanks, dumb blonds etc. All of them. Nice. <br><br>Anyway, I just cant see, again, what the author is TELLING us, that there is this uncontrollable undeniable attraction between Olivia and Caleb, that they MUST be together.<br><br><u>WHY</u> He didn’t like her enough to fight for in the beginning, and she didn’t really want him that much either, unless she was just playing hard to get and he missed the point and the whole scene just backfired on her. When they eventually get together in College, we lean that Caleb is very patient with Olivia over her <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[unwillingness or unreadyness to have sex. However, after they have planned a weekend away to consummate their relationship, Olivia walks in on Caleb about to cheat on her. He blames her, and doesn’t run after her (well, not quick enough if he did) and so Olivia does something equally rancid and picks up a random guy to have sex with. Caleb finds her in the hotel room they had planned to vacation in, and is sickend. He sees a condom wrapper on the nightstand, and Olivia then says that from that day forward he is never able to use a condom because of that memory – <b>HANG ON A MINUTE MISSUS??? DIDN’T HE GET HIS OTHER GIRLFRIEND PREGNANT??? LOOKS TO ME LIKE HE HAD AN AVERSION TO CONDOMS WAY BEFORE THEN!!!!!</b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=5b7nl2" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392487499ra/8568264.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Anyway, fast forward to the present, and again, I just don’t get it. Why did she not stay and fight for her man if she loved him the way we are TOLD she does, if she has the kind of ‘never go away” feelings we are TOLD she has?<br><br>MAKES NO SENSE<br><br>On and on into the story and we fast-forward several years. And AGAIN, they have a chance to be with each other; AGAIN neither of them clearly thinks the other is worth fighting for.<br><br>Even the scene in Rome, What.The.Fu*k????? <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=28bs4jr" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392487499i/8568265.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>There is NO explanation, and again, I fail to see their epic love when AGAIN Caleb does not see their love worth fighting for.<br><br>If a couple wanted to be together as much as we are TOLD these two do, they would fecking well fight tooth and nail to be together. <br><br><b>
  <u>BUT THEY DONT</u>
</b><br><br>As for the ending, well considering what went down in Rome, it seemed okay for Olivia. I genuinely wanted her to be happy and it seemed she had some closure on Caleb with that very last sentence.<br><br>Unfortunately not, fellow readers, there are two more books in this series.<br><br><b>I wanted this to be a Hell Yes, but it turned out to be another <u>SHell No</u>.</b><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16108484425396720204" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review830066379">

<div id="review_609112893" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/609112893" />
    <a title="Hershey " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19468761-hershey"><img alt="Hershey " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599546236p2/19468761.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/609112893?book_show_action=true">May 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hershey " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hershey " href="/user/show/19468761-hershey">Hershey </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19468761-hershey?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19468761-hershey?shelf=fun-fun-fun">fun-fun-fun</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19468761-hershey?shelf=quite-awesome">quite-awesome</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer609112893" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1787215898813745381"><b> Wow. Simply Fantabulous. </b><br/><br/>This book was a damn good roller coaster. I had an awesome jaw-dropping mind blowing heart wrenching ride.<br/><br/><b> <i> She cheated. She cheated for love. </i></b> <br/><br/><i> Olivia Kaspen </i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420652i/834694._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='600' alt=' photo 600full-raquel-alessi_zpsa150490e.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> "I was a relationship retard. I kicked, shoved, and punched people out my life, so they never had a chance to hurt me." - Olivia </i><br/><br/>Olivia Kaspen was a very complicated character to get into. She was so original which was really surprising because I hadn't come across such a scintillating character in a long time. H</span>
  <span id="freeText1787215898813745381" style="display:none"><b> Wow. Simply Fantabulous. </b><br><br>This book was a damn good roller coaster. I had an awesome jaw-dropping mind blowing heart wrenching ride.<br><br><b> <i> She cheated. She cheated for love. </i></b> <br><br><i> Olivia Kaspen </i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420652i/834694._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600" alt=" photo 600full-raquel-alessi_zpsa150490e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> "I was a relationship retard. I kicked, shoved, and punched people out my life, so they never had a chance to hurt me." - Olivia </i><br><br>Olivia Kaspen was a very complicated character to get into. She was so original which was really surprising because I hadn't come across such a scintillating character in a long time. Her originality kinda threw me off balance for a couple of chapters but then I got used to her. And then I started liking her narration which was really beautiful for such a wicked girl - ahem, <i> Desperately wicked </i> :D And then I fell in love with this book when Caleb was introduced.<br><br><i> Caleb Drake - The notorious Casanova :D :)</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418513i/828739._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Caleb was lovely. A perfect kinda boy. Olivia's and Caleb's romance was really cute. It was like a dream reading Olivia's versions of the the past and then the dream evaporated when the present was narrated. I liked the past till it collided with the present and then I loved the present. I'm sorry if I'm rambling here :D<br>Everybody has to wake up from their dreams at some point.<br><br>The Opportunist was an amazing book. It showed me how desperate people can get and at what lengths they could take their desperation. And Olivia's and Caleb's love was really perfect though they both messed it up. People are flawed, people cannot be predicted and I certainly couldn't predict Olivia which intrigued and captivated me even more.<br><br>I really couldn't say what I was feeling when I read this book. One minute I was content and grinning happily and the next minute I was like:<br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Like I mentioned earlier, this book was a good damn roller coaster. You never know when it's going to go upside down.<br><br>And in the end I made this terrible mistake of plugging my earphones on while reading the last few chapters. The roller coaster was coming to an end and I didn't want it to end because I really loved these two characters a lot, Olivia and Caleb. And alas the most poignant song I have in my music collection started playing...<br><br>We never realize what we have until its gone. That's how we are. Failing to realize. That's what happened in this book. Olivia didn't want to get hurt so she pushed people away not thinking how it might affect her later on. Many of us do that too. We push certain things away and then later on we cry realizing we took it for granted and begging the universe to give it back.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/625904.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Olivia was a good person but was all too messed up with her emotions. I guess she found solace in revenge. Revenge is such a cruel thing and how it spoils our mind within seconds. Olivia's actions were sometimes confounding and I don't think I can ever judge her for all her actions. Her actions for the moment felt right somehow even though later on I might end up rolling my eyes or scrunching my face :D<br><br>In the end, everything was very unexpected. I found it difficult to part with this book because it is ever so rare that I like <i> roller coasters </i> and this one was marvelous. <br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><b> The best roller coaster ride ever! </b><br> </span>
  <a data-text-id="1787215898813745381" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_338366016" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/338366016" />
    <a title="Lisa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8179357-lisa"><img alt="Lisa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346526379p2/8179357.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/338366016?book_show_action=true">May 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa" href="/user/show/8179357-lisa">Lisa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8179357-lisa?shelf=loved">loved</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer338366016" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11891827073803277288">Still my favorite book of the year, if not ever;)<br/><br/>Tarryn Fisher is a literary genius! I love her angst-filled, totally unpredictable writing style. This is hands down one of the best books I have read this year if not ever!<br/><br/>When I finished this book, I literally wept for a good 15 minutes and was teary eyed off and on well until now (finished it Tuesday afternoon). I tried to go to sleep last night but couldn't stop thinking about The Opportunist, I got up in the middle of the night to feed my new</span>
  <span id="freeText11891827073803277288" style="display:none">Still my favorite book of the year, if not ever;)<br /><br />Tarryn Fisher is a literary genius! I love her angst-filled, totally unpredictable writing style. This is hands down one of the best books I have read this year if not ever!<br /><br />When I finished this book, I literally wept for a good 15 minutes and was teary eyed off and on well until now (finished it Tuesday afternoon). I tried to go to sleep last night but couldn't stop thinking about The Opportunist, I got up in the middle of the night to feed my newborn and I thought of The Opportunist, and when I woke this morning, the first thing I thought about again was The Opportunist. It was sexy, exciting, frustrating, sad and and I feel like I just took my car too fast down a Lombard Street of emotion and then forgot about the stop sign at the bottom! You REALLY, REALLY need to read this if you haven't already!<br /><br />Caleb and Olivia, they make me want to scream at the top of my lungs. Don't get me wrong, I loved them, then I furious at one or both, and then I loved them again but they both sucked at seizing the day. How many times would a little honesty have brought them together or kept them together? Both could have done better by the other and there was a lot of irony in how pendulum swung between who was currently at fault for their troubles. I thought Caleb could do no wrong and then he did and I thought I would end the book hating Olivia but I loved her.<br /><br />Caleb is a romantic, slightly alpha male with a British accent. I think I have mentioned before that I love men with British accents! He compared Olivia to a llama and a heeled boot and made it all sound so sexy! What he did to earn his first date with Olivia was beyond hot and original and I immediately fell in love with him! Olivia is a bruised soul; she really lacks the capacity to let herself feel and be in love. I wanted to shake her and tell her to open her eyes to see what was standing right in front of her! She blamed herself for a little more than I thought she should and convinced herself that she was not worthy of the knock your socks off type of love she was getting from Caleb. When they are together, I felt the fire, compatibility and endless love but when they are apart, I felt torn, incomplete and sad. They are soul mates and I cannot imagine them ever being truly happy without each other.<br /><br />And Leah, at this point, I want to pull you by your red hair and make you confess to all the things you have done to manipulate fate! Uhhh, I just don't see myself ever truly liking you unless you come clean and let whatever happens happen! Can you work on that in book #2 Leah? Please?<br /><br />I need to share one of my favorite lines from the book as there were some great ones. This one melts me every time I read it... "It is the last real kiss of my life. I forever cling to that kiss. It was goodbye and I'm sorry and I love you so much." *Crying*<br /><br />Oh, and then there was this one... "You can only give your heart away once, after that, everything else will chase your first love."<br /><br />Uhh, Tarryn Fisher, I love you!<br /><br />There is really so much I would like to say in addition to this but since my hope is you take your own ride down Lombard Street, I don't want to let you know where all the curves are. <br /><br />It is a book that will stick with me for a long time. I cannot wait for book two which looks like it will be released around April 2013 and will be titled Dirty Red (title suits Leah just fine!). In the meantime, I may have to find a The Opportunist support group to deal with my addiction and ongoing hangover! Oh hell, just writing this review has restored some of my happy.<br /> <br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="11891827073803277288" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/317046126?book_show_action=true">Apr 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Calia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Calia" href="/user/show/5918467-calia">Calia</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer317046126" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer14175128476419510440">How.. I can't even right now. How does one rate this book?!!? Tarryn... what did you do to me!??!?!<br/><br/><b>EDIT: May 23rd,2012</b> <br/><u>7 Stages of Grief..</u> <br/><br/><b>1.</b> <u>Shock and Denial.</u> <br/>Mine hit the minute I finished reading the book. I walked away.... pretended it didn't end that way. I conjured up what I really wanted to happen. I read that the denial in grief can weeks to get over.... God help me. <br/><br/><b>2.</b> <u>Pain and Guilt</u> Haven't had that yet.... let's give it time goodfriends. <br/><br/><b>3.</b> <u>Anger and Bargaining</u><br/>I'm still going through </span>
  <span id="freeText14175128476419510440" style="display:none">How.. I can't even right now. How does one rate this book?!!? Tarryn... what did you do to me!??!?!<br /><br /><b>EDIT: May 23rd,2012</b> <br /><u>7 Stages of Grief..</u> <br /><br /><b>1.</b> <u>Shock and Denial.</u> <br />Mine hit the minute I finished reading the book. I walked away.... pretended it didn't end that way. I conjured up what I really wanted to happen. I read that the denial in grief can weeks to get over.... God help me. <br /><br /><b>2.</b> <u>Pain and Guilt</u> Haven't had that yet.... let's give it time goodfriends. <br /><br /><b>3.</b> <u>Anger and Bargaining</u><br />I'm still going through this....I want to lash out at something. But then I realize "Oh crap, it's just a book." But then I think.. "No.. it's more than a book! Ms. Fisher is an emotional brain ninja!!" <br /><br />Follow me through my 7 stages of grieving <i>The Opportunist</i>....<br /><br /><b>EDIT:May 26th,2012</b><br />I'm still grieving. <br />My anger is still there. But let's be clear. It's not anger over Olivia. In fact I was quite smitten with her. <br />Although... <i>Leah</i> PFT!PFT! (that's the french way for spitting.) I still get a tick in my eye when I think about her. And when I think about book 2. I hope the first scene starts out with her leaving Neiman Marcus and getting hit by a cab... <i>What?? Is that too much anger?!</i> or someone clubbing her with a pair of <i>Louboutin's</i> <br /><br /><b>4.</b> <u>The Upside</u> <br />What's the upside of this book? What's NOT the upside? Good grief this lady can write. Scenes with Caleb and Olivia are ahhh-mazing! Especially their scenes from the past.<br />I'm not the first one to mentions this.. But the basketball game scene?! I knew right then and there that Olivia was going to be marked as <b>"One of my favorite Main Characters"</b><br /><br /><b>5.</b> <u> Acceptance</u><br />I've accepted that this book is <b>incredible.</b> And even though Ms. Fisher shredded my emotions like a cheese grater.... I love this book. <br />Also, I'm a sucker for a good cover. And this cover? <u>Looks completely like Olivia.</u> Freakishly good hair and all...<br /><br />Okay, so I didn't have <b>ALL</b> 7 stages of grief. But I hit 5 out of 7. <br />And that my friends is what I like to call a mind-blowing novel.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1161504181931372474"><br/>Throughout this book I kept repeating one line over and over again... <br/><br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/oh%20hell%20no/demony1999/tumblr_m5ex9zS1xy1rqymef.gif?o=18' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/591075.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Ok so it was actually <b> OH HELL NO!</b> <i> but I liked this gif lol</i> <br/><br/>What a psychological mind fuck of a book! <b> IT WAS FUCKING AWESOME!</b> <br/>I devoured it... Could not get enough of it, when I wasn't reading I was obsessing about when I could read next! <br/><br/>I loved the past and pretense that this book had, I loved the characters. I hated the characters. I hated myself for loving then hating them. Ugh it's just AMAZING. <br/><br/>I don't think I can </span>
  <span id="freeText1161504181931372474" style="display:none"><br>Throughout this book I kept repeating one line over and over again... <br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/oh%20hell%20no/demony1999/tumblr_m5ex9zS1xy1rqymef.gif?o=18" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer594118986" class="readable"
